British Foreign Secretary Announces Arms Embargo on Italy and Abyssinia, Japan Also Imposes Embargo on Abyssinia

(London) British Foreign Secretary Hoare stated in the House of Commons today that British military supplies destined for Italy or Abyssinia will not be issued export licenses for the time being. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

(London) British Foreign Secretary Hoare today made a long-awaited statement in the House of Commons regarding the export of arms, saying that Britain will temporarily not issue export licenses for arms to Italy and Abyssinia. However, according to Article 9 of the treaty of August 21, 1930, military supplies destined for Abyssinia that pass through British territory or British protectorates may be allowed to pass. Reuters has learned that the British government's position is to continue its efforts to achieve a round table conference and discuss a peaceful resolution to the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. However, if these efforts are unsuccessful, the British government will discuss the issue of arms embargoes with other countries to reach a decision. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Beijing The Belgian government today decided to prohibit the shipment of chemical weapons to Abyssinia. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

(Tokyo) A Foreign Ministry spokesperson announced that the Japanese government has not issued passports for the transportation of military supplies to Abyssinia. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

France Expresses Its Attitude: Laval Reports to the Government

(Paris) At today's State Council meeting, Premier and Foreign Minister Laval reported on the recent negotiations among the governments of Britain, France, Italy, and Abyssinia to seek a way to peacefully resolve the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. Laval then outlined the attitude that France should adopt when the League of Nations Council convenes next week, which the State Council approved. The attitude France should adopt is to try in many ways to avoid harming its friendship with Italy and its friendship with Britain, while also adhering to the principles of the League of Nations. However, the French government's position on solutions is not rigid and unchangeable. Laval will likely not hold a fixed preconception when he leaves for Geneva. The date of the League of Nations Council meeting is currently unknown. This Council meeting is at the urging of the British side. If the parties concerned can agree on a solution before the meeting, then there is no need for the Council to meet. However, this hope is rather unexpected and unlikely. Since the Italian government recently sent a note to Abyssinia, the situation has improved slightly. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini stated in the note that if the border issue could be avoided and the fifth neutral arbitrator did not have to be appointed, then the reconciliation process stipulated in the 1928 Italo-Abyssinian treaty could continue. The Abyssinian Emperor believes that since Italy and Abyssinia have failed to reach a compromise, the League of Nations should step in to handle the matter impartially. If the fifth neutral arbitrator cannot be appointed, then the League of Nations should, in accordance with the procedures stipulated in Article 15 of the Covenant, conduct a full discussion of the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. Although the positions of Italy and Abyssinia are incompatible, there may still be room for compromise on the appointment of the fifth neutral arbitrator. Talks between the governments of Britain, France, Italy, and Abyssinia will continue until the Council meeting. The circumstances of the Council's discussion may change completely due to these talks between the four countries. Today, Laval will also meet with British Ambassador to France, Sir Clerk. All matters will be discussed. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

League of Nations Meeting at End of Month: Britain and France Still Disagree on Policy

(Geneva) Due to the inability to appoint the fifth arbitrator in a timely manner, it is expected that the League of Nations Council meeting to consider the Italo-Abyssinian dispute will be convened on July 31. Britain and France have not yet agreed on the policy to be adopted by the Council. The French government still hopes that the discussion will be limited to the border conflict issue and that the fifth arbitrator can be appointed, so that the consideration of the overall case can be postponed to late August. However, according to various sources, Britain will be prepared to deal with a frank discussion of the whole problem and to follow the natural path of Abyssinia's petition in accordance with Article 15 of the League Covenant. It is expected that Britain's position will be supported by the Little Entente, the Balkan Entente, and the majority of the League of Nations members. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) Premier Laval and League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol have agreed that the League of Nations Council will meet next week to discuss the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. Avenol will notify Council Chairman Litvinov by telephone after returning to Geneva to determine the definite date of the meeting. It is predicted that the meeting will likely be held on July 30 or 31, and that the debate will not extend to August 3. Unless special circumstances arise, Laval will personally lead the French delegation to the meeting. Litvinov is expected to arrive here today. Litvinov will consult with Laval on all matters before going to Geneva. It is unanimously hoped that this meeting will have sufficient success in discussing the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, so that it will not be necessary to hold another meeting in mid-August as previously planned. Since Article 15 of the League Covenant is the main basis for discussion, the League of Nations Council may ask Italy and Abyssinia to reach a settlement themselves, so that the League of Nations can avoid continuing to discuss this dispute. (National Telegraph dispatch, 25th)

(London) Britain today firmly defended the authority of the League of Nations in order to save the opportunity for war between Italy and Abyssinia. Soviet Russia has expressed its support for Britain's proposal to use the League of Nations as a tool for peace. The developments in the Italo-Abyssinian situation can be summarized as follows:

(1) Britain reiterated its opposition to the League of Nations ignoring the matter.

(2) Foreign Secretary Hoare assured Parliament that the government is prepared to cooperate with the United States to maintain peace.

(3) Soviet Russia and Turkey advocate exerting the authority of the League of Nations, even if it means forcing Italy to withdraw from the League of Nations.

(4) Insurers are no longer accepting war insurance for East Africa.

(5) Britain denied the rumor that it would continue to send troops to Africa. According to Geneva sources, the League of Nations Secretary-General will submit a report to the Council meeting next week, stating that Japan is currently transporting large quantities of military supplies to Abyssinia via Djibouti in French Somaliland. Observers generally believe that Japan's move will put France in a dilemma. (National Telegraph dispatch, 25th)

British Labor Circles Oppose Italy: Hold General Meeting and Pass Resolution

(London) The National Labor Federation, jointly organized by the Labor Party Executive Committee, the Labor Party Parliamentary Group, and the British Trades Union Congress, recently held a meeting here to discuss the Italo-Abyssinian issue and passed a resolution. The gist of the resolution stated that "Italian Fascists are trying to deceive the people and make them take risky actions in Africa in the hope of unattainable glory, thereby saving the domestic economic, financial, political, and cultural decline. However, in reality, the various disputes cited by Italy are not significant in nature and have little relevance. They should not cause turmoil and unrest in Africa. Furthermore, the Covenant of the League of Nations and the Kellogg-Briand Pact have become the new international code followed by countries around the world, and the foundation of European peace is also built on these two conventions. Now, because of the Italo-Abyssinian issue, this new international code is in danger of collapsing, and European peace is also in imminent danger. Therefore, the National Labor Federation specifically requests the government to immediately propose, when the League of Nations Council meets, that the Council determine the responsibilities of both Italy and Abyssinia in accordance with the Covenant, and clearly declare that Britain will bear all the obligations and responsibilities that a member state of the League of Nations should bear, without partiality or fear. The League of Nations Council should also, in accordance with Abyssinia's request, immediately send neutral observers to the Abyssinian border to investigate the truth of the dispute. Any person who engages in the slaughter of the African people in pursuit of the glory of a new fascist empire should be prohibited from lending any money. It should be known that the path to a peaceful solution does not lie in forcing Abyssinia to submit to fascist Italy, but in making fascist Italy realize that popular anger is insurmountable, and that it will not dare to act against the great displeasure of the world." (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Italian Newspapers Stop Anti-Japanese Reports

(Rome) Italian newspapers have been publishing fierce commentaries attacking Japan in recent days. However, as of the 24th, all newspapers in the country uniformly stopped publishing news and commentaries attacking Japan. The reason seems to be that Mussolini realized the disadvantage of attacking Japan and issued a ban. (Japanese United News dispatch, 24th)

(Tokyo) Tokyo Army authorities today spoke about the rumors of Japanese military equipment being transported to Abyssinia, saying that there are various irresponsible rumors about this matter, and their purpose is obviously to involve Japan in the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. However, the Army authorities neither admitted nor denied whether it was true that Japan was supplying Abyssinia with military equipment, but said that they did not see the need to explain whether Japan was exporting military equipment to Abyssinia or not. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

London Air Defense Drill: Authorities Announce Defense is Strong

(London) London held an air raid drill from 6:00 PM last night to 8:00 AM this morning, which has just ended. According to authorities, London's defenses are strong and cannot be breached by air raids. The defenders inflicted heavy losses on the attacking side. The attackers consisted of eight squadrons of bombers. Only one entire squadron completely escaped the defenders. This morning, during the general attack by the eight squadrons, seven of them were intercepted by the defenders. (Reuters dispatch, 24th)

Instability in Dutch Politics: Cabinet Considers Resignation

The Hague Efforts to prevent a cabinet crisis are currently underway behind the scenes, as there are fears of unexpected consequences if one occurs. However, the issue of the cabinet's resignation remains highly possible, as merchants are generally dissatisfied with its firm policy of maintaining the gold standard. Even if the Colijn cabinet resigns, as he is the most respected figure in the country, he will eventually have to return to power sooner or later. According to general observation, the formation of an alliance between the Catholic Party and the Socialist Party is unlikely, as under the current circumstances, the Catholic Party has no other intention than to cooperate with the Colijn Party. Therefore, even if Colijn resigns, the person who forms the new government will undoubtedly be Colijn. According to reliable sources, the Queen seems to be consulting with Colijn again before making a decision on policy. However, some believe that dissolving Parliament and holding new elections is another option after the cabinet resigns. The Dutch Bank and the Dutch government are currently taking all necessary measures to try to maintain the Dutch currency. About seven million gold pounds of gold reserves were proposed to be withdrawn by Britain and France last week. (National Telegraph dispatch, 25th)

The Hague According to an official announcement, the Colijn government has not yet resigned, but is considering whether to resign or dissolve Parliament. At the same time, the cabinet will continue to be responsible and will adhere to its policy implemented so far, which is to strive to protect the Dutch currency. If necessary, it will immediately take emergency measures to avoid attacks from all sides. Premier Colijn met with the Queen this afternoon and afterward declared to the political world that the Queen refused to accept the cabinet's resignation. However, how this matter is studied will depend on the developments tomorrow. (National Telegraph dispatch, 24th)

Division Within the American Silver Bloc: Issue of Repealing the Profits Tax

(Washington) A division was discovered among the American silver bloc members today. They said that the silver bloc was not bound by any agreement. Pittman is involved in the Western silver mine merger and can no longer be the spokesman for the silver bloc. It is expected that when Thomas presents his views to the Senate on repealing the silver profit tax, the issue of destroying the previous agreement will continue to be discussed. At that time, Thomas will describe the entire situation in detail. President Roosevelt told reporters this afternoon that he was preparing to reply to a letter from the silver bloc and some of its members, but he did not say how he would reply. Austria Arrests 500 National Socialists: Anniversary of Prime Minister's Assassination

(Vienna) Today marks the first anniversary of the assassination of former Prime Minister Dollfuss. To prevent disturbances, the police authorities arrested 500 National Socialists and placed them under "protective detention". All public offices and homeowners flew black flags until midnight today to express their condolences. The flags were raised from noon yesterday until midnight today. Last night, for one hour, candles were lit in all windows in Vienna to pay tribute to the former Prime Minister, a scene of tranquility that saddened those who saw it. A large-scale memorial service will be held here today. Churches in London and Rome will also hold memorial services. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Japanese Ministry of Communications' Plan to Train Pilots

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Communications' ten-year plan for developing aviation has been formally decided by the Aviation Business Committee. The most important part of this plan is the training of aviation personnel. According to this plan, 400 first-class pilots, 1,000 second-class pilots, and 300 engineers will be trained in ten years. Because the Ministry of Communications relies on the Army and Navy for training, it is insufficient to meet the needs. It intends to establish its own training institutions dedicated to this work. (Japanese United News dispatch, 25th)

Chinese Artifacts Arrive in England: Exhibition in November, Queen to Open

(London) The British cruiser HMS Suffolk, which departed from Shanghai on June 7 carrying precious Chinese art for the International Art Exhibition at Burlington House this winter, arrived in Portsmouth today. Dr. Chen, Counselor of the Chinese Embassy, Sir Casry, Keeper of Documents at the Foreign Office, and Mr. Lyme, Secretary of the Royal Academy of Arts, traveled by car to Portsmouth to greet the ship. The three boarded the ship and had lunch with Captain Manners. They then inspected the hundred steel-clad boxes containing the treasures being unloaded onto three freight cars and a motor truck. The unloading was handled by a commercial firm with extensive experience in transporting treasures from France, Italy, the Netherlands, and Persia to Burlington House for exhibition. The freight cars transporting the treasures are expected to arrive in London at 8:00 PM tonight. Armed police will be stationed on the freight cars, and police officers will accompany them in cars for escort. Zheng Tianxi, a member of the Chinese Exhibition Committee, will monitor the boxes being moved from the cars to the Royal Academy of Arts' warehouse. The boxes will be opened after Chinese packaging experts arrive here in September. The amount of insurance for the treasures is still unknown, as there is no need for insurance during the voyage from Shanghai to London on a British warship. However, the British government is currently handling insurance matters. It is hoped that the Queen will personally attend the opening ceremony of the exhibition in November. The Queen is very interested in Chinese art and is an expert. She will likely exhibit some of her own treasures along with the exhibits. Chinese Ambassador Guo Taiqi and his wife were received by the Queen on July 20. The Queen received them in the Chinese Room, which is divided into two large rooms filled with ancient Chinese paintings, porcelains, and bronzes. The Queen discussed Chinese art with Ambassador Guo and his wife for a long time and pointed out the items she had purchased herself. The United States and the Netherlands will also send treasures to the exhibition. Several French, German, and private collectors may also participate. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

—Special Commercial Report by Reuters on July 25—

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today is 140 shillings and 9 pence, up 3 pence.

London Silver Market: Today it is stable, the price is unchanged. Spot price remains at 30 pence 1875, futures at 30 pence 325. The U.S. government and Indian speculators are buying, while China and speculators are selling.

Mount Isa Silver: Futures opened quietly, with the September contract falling £5, to 68.00-68.25.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was rather quiet this morning. The French exchange rate was subject to adjustment by the authorities. The opening price for British-American exchange was 4 dollars, 9 cents, 5 minutes, 56 5, lower than yesterday's closing price by 0.0625. Within the first hour, it rose by 0.0625, fell again by 0.0625 at noon, and rose by 25 at 2 PM, to 4 dollars, 9 cents, 5 minutes, 8125, higher than the opening price by 25.

British-French: The opening price was 74 francs 94, down £2. At 1 PM, it rose by £3, to 74 francs 97. At 2 PM, it rose again by £7, reaching 75 francs 04, higher than the opening price by £10.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: Opening was quiet and unremarkable, due to the Senate passing an amendment to the Agricultural Adjustment Act without including export subsidy clauses, causing uncertainty in the cotton market. Opening prices were lower than yesterday's closing, but market prices fluctuated minimally before noon due to a lack of interest.

Chicago Wheat Market: Opening was quiet, with prices slightly lower. Grain prices remained unchanged. Soon after, both wheat and grain prices rose by about a third.

Liverpool Wheat Market: Today's prices plummeted. At 1 PM, the October futures price was 5 shillings even, down 1 pence 875.

Liverpool Cotton Market: Today it was firmer. At 1 PM, the October futures price was 6.3, up £5.

Rubber

London: Today's opening was stable, then turned quiet. At noon, October and December futures were at 5 pence 75, the same as yesterday's closing price.

New York: Today it soared, due to rumors in London and New York that the International Rubber Regulation Committee will meet soon. Opening prices were about £6 higher than yesterday's closing. The trend was upward before noon.

Securities

New York: Today's opening was stable, but several stocks lagged slightly. Later, due to cautious observation by merchants, the market showed a mixed picture. The average price of the Dow Jones 30 industrial stocks opened at 24.63, up £3. The New York stock market prices are listed on the left.

Chairman Chiang's Instructions: The Meaning of the National Flag and the Essentials of the New Life Movement

—Chengdu Extends Commemorative Week and Expands Propaganda Meeting for the New Life Movement—

Chengdu Correspondence: At 9 AM on the 15th, Chairman Chiang Zhuang Rong 7 [character unclear] held an expanded Commemorative Week and the Chengdu New Life Movement expanded propaganda meeting at the Shaocheng Park Sports Ground. Attending were Chairman Chiang, Chairman Liu, staff of the Generalissimo's Headquarters, generals of various armies, various party, government, and military organizations, various schools, various mass organizations, and the city's boy scouts and military training students, totaling approximately 20,000 people. After Chairman Chiang led the flag-raising ceremony, he delivered a political speech, the words of which are as follows: "Chairman Liu, Comrades from all circles, Compatriots, today our comrades and compatriots from all circles in Chengdu are gathered in Shaocheng Park to hold the Premier's Commemorative Week, and before the Commemorative Week, we are holding a flag-raising ceremony. Everyone must know the meaning of the national flag and its relationship to our nation and people, which is very important. Therefore, I want to take this opportunity to first tell everyone the meaning of our national flag. The national flag is the sacred symbol representing the country, so we, the citizens of the Republic of China, must first recognize our national flag if we want to recognize our country. If we don't even recognize our own national flag clearly, then we won't have a concept of the country, and of course, we can't love the country. Now, foreigners, whether they are three-year-old children, all recognize their national flags and understand the meaning of their national flags. Therefore, everyone can love the country and sacrifice for the country. However, among our 400 million compatriots in China, very few people truly know the meaning of the national flag. Therefore, the national concept of the general public is extremely weak. Many people hardly know what the national flag is, let alone how to love the country. Therefore, the country is being oppressed and invaded by others day by day, leading to the current critical state of survival. Therefore, in the future, we must make all the people of the country recognize the country and work hard to save the country, and we must first make every compatriot able to recognize and love the national flag that represents the country. The national flag is not only the sacred symbol representing the country, but also the place where the spirit and life of our Han nation, from our ancestor the Yellow Emperor to us and future generations for thousands of years, are concentrated and entrusted. Therefore, the honor and disgrace of the national flag can reflect the rise and fall, honor and disgrace of our entire country and nation. The current style of our Republic of China's national flag, called the 'Blue Sky, White Sun, and Red Earth,' was created by our Premier, who led the revolutionary party—the Kuomintang—when it first rose up to overthrow the Manchu Qing. Because the Manchu Qing was the enemy of our country and nation, invading our China 300 years ago, occupying our Chinese land, and oppressing our 400 million Chinese compatriots, so that 'the majestic Chinese nation was not worthy of the ranks of nations, and the flourishing clothing and hats were despised by foreign tribes.' The foreign flag—the former dragon flag—flew in our China for more than 200 years. The alien government oppressed our people's national thought, extinguished our people's national spirit, and did not allow our people to personally love the country and value the nation. Because such oppression lasted too long, many of our people still do not know that they have their own country and nation, only knowing their own family, not knowing the country, which is our big family. Only with a country can there be a home, and only with a home can there be a self. Therefore, to protect one's own family, one must first protect the country. If the country is destroyed, one's own family cannot be protected, and one's own self will become a slave or livestock of others. They will beat you when they want to beat you, and kill you when they want to kill you, as the saying goes, 'People are the knife and chopping board, and I am the fish and meat.' At that time, we will have no sovereignty at all, what kind of person would we be? Our Premier, in order to wash away more than 200 years of [character unclear] shameful humiliation, relieve the pain of alien oppression, awaken the national concept and national spirit of all compatriots, and revitalize our 5,000-year-old civilized country, rose up in revolution, overthrew the Manchu Qing, and replaced the dragon flag with the 'Blue Sky, White Sun, and Red Earth' national flag. When the 'Blue Sky, White Sun, and Red Earth' national flag began to rise, it was the time when our nation and people had the supreme independent personality, and began to be independent and free. In other words, the Blue Sky, White Sun, and Red Earth' national flag is the concrete symbol of the independent and free Republic of China. Therefore, the Blue Sky, White Sun, and Red Earth' national flag is the soul that our Chinese nation, from the Yellow Emperor to our ancestors and Premier, and the general revolutionary martyrs, has entrusted to, and it is also the gathering place of the common faith of our 400 million compatriots. Therefore, if we want to respect our ancestors and love our country, we must respect the national flag and love the national flag. Respecting the national flag and loving the national flag is respecting our ancestors and loving our country. When we see the national flag, it is like seeing our country and ancestors, as well as the martyrs who sacrificed for the revolution since the Premier, and we should stand in awe and rise up in excitement. We must continue to maintain and carry forward the great national life and culture of our ancestors for 5,000 years, save our country, revitalize our nation, and make the national flag forever fly in the world. This is the meaning that our 400 million people, especially the general young compatriots, should clearly recognize and the responsibility they should bear. This is speaking about the vertical meaning of the national flag. Secondly, I will talk about the horizontal meaning of the national flag. Everyone must know why our Republic of China's national flag is designed as 'Blue Sky, White Sun, and Red Earth.' This is because our Premier, based on the meaning of 'the world is for the public' and 'all people are equal,' determined it. He used the blue sky and white sun to represent our country, not only wanting our country to be as new as the blue sky and white sun, and to exist permanently in the universe, but also to shine like the sun in the sky, universally illuminating the whole world, making the whole world bright everywhere, and forever bright, creating a new world of freedom, equality, civilization, and peace where the world is for the public. This is a long-term and bright goal indicated by the Premier for our country, and it is also the long-term responsibility of our 400 million people, especially the general young compatriots. Therefore, we should strive to be strong and strive to be heroes to save our country and revitalize our nation, so that our country will become the master of world peace, and promote our national history and culture to benefit the whole world. Speaking of this, there is still one point to add, that is, the twelve rays of the white sun symbolize the eleven [typo, should be twelve] hours of each day and the eleven months of each year. The meaning is that we, like the earth, can continuously progress day and night, year after year, constantly striving for progress, which is the meaning of 'constantly striving for self-improvement like the heavens.' Everyone must know that there is absolutely no person or country in the world that can avoid defeat and destruction if they are lazy, corrupt, and decadent. Only by constantly striving for self-improvement can we, as individuals, succeed in our careers, create a new life for ourselves, and fulfill our responsibilities to the nation and people. As for the nation and people, we can independently survive, create a new life for the nation and people, and achieve the great mission that our Republic of China should bear to the world. The above is an explanation of the vertical and horizontal meaning of the 'form' of the national flag. Below, I will briefly talk about the meaning of the 'color' of the national flag. Generally speaking, the color of the blue sky symbolizes freedom, the color of the white sun symbolizes equality, and the color of the red earth symbolizes universal love. It is very painful for a person to be oppressed in a dark and hopeless situation. Seeing the blue sky and white sun is like coming out of the darkness, and the so-called 'seeing the light of day again' is a very happy thing. This is true for an individual, and the same is true for a nation. Now our nation is being invaded and oppressed, and the danger and pain can be said to have reached the extreme. The national flag instructs our 400 million compatriots to be determined to strive to save the country and achieve a position of freedom and equality, and to create a new China with complete sovereignty and a truly independent personality. And we must use the great benevolence of saving people and teaching the world to save the suffering masses and small and weak nations in the world, so that they can share the happiness of freedom, equality, and peace with us. But how can we achieve this goal of saving the country and saving the world? This all depends on the soundness of our 400 million compatriots. In this regard, the three colors of the national flag have extremely important instructions. The color of the blue sky indicates that our Chinese people should have lofty and great aspirations, the color of the white sun shows that our Chinese people should have a bright and pure heart and mind, and the color of the red earth indicates that our Chinese people should have a warm spirit of sacrifice. If a person has lofty and great aspirations, a bright and pure heart, and a brave and striving spirit of sacrifice for the nation, he will surely become a sage or hero, do a revolutionary cause for society and the country, and be praised and admired by the world and future generations. Conversely, if he has a little selfishness, meanness, baseness, cowardice, and decadence, then he cannot become a sage or hero, and is not worthy of being a citizen of the Republic of China. The red color of the national flag symbolizes the blood of the martyrs who have lofty and great aspirations and pure hearts, and who fought and sacrificed for the freedom and equality of the nation and the salvation of the suffering people. Therefore, the red color of the national flag can be said to be dyed with the immeasurable red blood shed by the martyrs. In the future, if we want to save the country and revitalize it, and strive for the freedom and equality of the nation, and create a solemn and brilliant new country, we must continue the spirit of our martyrs, follow the path of blood of our martyrs, and spill our full cavity of red [character unclear] blood for the nation. [Character unclear] For three hundred years, our ancestors and martyrs, our ancestors, sacrificed many lives and shed much blood to dye the solemn and brilliant national flag as it is now. The souls of our Premier and the ancestors and martyrs who sacrificed for the nation are entrusted to this national flag and flutter above our heads, increasing the status and glory of our nation. Therefore, all of us, up and down the country, all descendants of the Yellow Emperor, should especially love the national flag with sincerity, and maintain the national flag with hot blood. The insult of the national flag is our insult, and the glory of the national flag is our glory. We would rather sacrifice everything personal, and absolutely not allow the national flag to be insulted in the slightest. We must know that what the national flag represents is the Republic of China, and the Republic of China is the country of our 400 million people. Our 400 million compatriots must be as close as hands and feet, love each other, be of one heart and one mind, and work together to protect our country and promote our nation. Therefore, the first requirement for saving the country and revitalizing it is that all compatriots in the country help each other, cooperate with each other, be sincerely united, gather the hearts of all the people of the country into one heart, and combine the strength of the country into one force, to strive for survival for the nation and to strive for glory for the country. In this way, we will not be ashamed to be the filial sons and virtuous grandsons of the Yellow Emperor, the true believers of the Premier, and the upright citizens of the Republic of China. Finally, regarding the essentials of the New Life Movement, I have been talking about it a lot in the past two years. You can understand it by reading the books on the New Life Movement. Today, I don't need to say more. In short, the New Life Movement is an easy, basic, and most important method of saving the country. As mentioned earlier, everyone should understand the meaning of the national flag and respect and love the national flag, and protect their compatriots and cooperate with each other to unite as one. This is the most important starting point for practicing the New Life Movement. If you don't know how to respect and love the country, and you can't love and cooperate with your compatriots, then you are not worthy of being a modern citizen of the Republic of China. As for the fundamental spirit of the New Life Movement, it lies in restoring the inherent virtues of etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame that have been passed down by our people for five thousand years. The ancients said, "Etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the four dimensions of a country. If the four dimensions are not established, the country will perish." The reason why our nation is so dangerous today is because we have lost etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Now, if we want to save the country and revitalize the nation, we must first restore the four dimensions. If the four dimensions can be restored, the country will surely be saved and the nation will surely be revitalized. Therefore, I often say, "Etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the four dimensions of a country. If the four dimensions are established, the country will be revived." If we want to practice etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame, we must start from daily life. All aspects of food, clothing, housing, and transportation must conform to etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame. "Etiquette" is a proper attitude and orderly and solemn action. Today, our holding of the Commemorative Week and the flag-raising ceremony is a manifestation of etiquette. With etiquette, we can understand righteousness, observe integrity, and know shame. Therefore, everyone should pay special attention to etiquette, not only to parents and elders should be [character unclear] polite, but also to all comrades and all compatriots should be polite to each other and love each other. In addition, all things must be done properly, clearly distinguished, and truly understood, in order to be considered as practicing the New Life. If all 400 million compatriots in the country [character unclear] can do this, they can become modern citizens and create a civilized and ethical country. Especially the general youth, must do this [character unclear] point, so that they can make contributions to the country and not be ashamed to be the masters of the country in the future. Not only should you practice the New Life yourself, but also hope that you will lead by example and influence everyone you come into contact with, so that everyone can practice the New Life. All 400 million compatriots in the country [character unclear] can unify their will [character unclear], unite their spirit, concentrate their strength, prepare hot blood, and work together to win a breath for the nation. In this way, our country will surely be saved and the nation will surely be revitalized. This is everyone's duty. It is hoped that in accordance with the principles of neatness, cleanliness, simplicity, plainness, speed, and certainty of the New Life, we will work together and earnestly do it to become a citizen of your new era." (July 18)

Qin Fen Reports on the River Defense Situation

Dredging Water and Dyke Breaches All Instructed for Defense; Project Funds Also Being Released Gradually

Beijing News: Qin Fen, Secretary-General of the Economic Commission, attended the Executive Yuan's routine meeting yesterday morning and reported in detail on the recent flood control situation of the Yangtze and Fei Rivers. The content of his flood control report is roughly as follows:

Yangtze River Flood Control: Water Level Rising

It has been found that since the beginning of July this year, there has been continuous heavy rainfall in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, resulting in a sharp rise in water levels in various places upstream. The water level height has even broken past records for the same period, and in some cases, exceeded the highest flood level in the past twenty years. The water levels in the downstream areas have also increased rapidly. At the same time, the Xiang River water level has also risen, causing the Yangtze River embankments to be under extreme pressure. Since the beginning of July, reports of embankment emergencies have been pouring in from all sides. The commission has issued instructions for protection and rescue based on the reported emergencies and overflows.

Gan (Jiangxi) and E (Hubei) Embankments: Rescue Measures

The dangerous situations of each embankment and the additional protection measures instructed by the commission are briefly described as follows: (1) The Guangcheng Wei Haikou Zhou in Anhui Province breached. The commission sent engineer Dong Wenqi to inspect the site and guide the rescue. (2) The Yu Jiapu section of the Ma Hua Dike in Jiangxi Province breached, with a breach width of 380 meters. Qin Fen and others departed on July 7th to inspect the Yangtze River water situation. On their way through Anhui Province, they consulted with Chairman Liu Zhenhua and agreed on a construction project to be directed and supervised by the Yangtze River Commission, with the Director of the Anhui Construction Department serving as the head of the engineering office. They are currently purchasing materials and actively recruiting workers. (3) The A, Gongchu, and Tongren embankments in Jiangxi Province are sinking. The Yangtze River Commission team leader Yang Jian is currently overseeing the efforts of 800 civilians from Jiujiang County and others to vigorously rescue them. As of the 18th, they are still not out of danger. (4) The Deshengtai section of the Jingjiang Dike in Hubei Province was reported to have been scoured by a 50-zhang (approximately 167 meters) long and 8-9 chi (approximately 2.7-3 meters) deep washout. The commission has instructed the Jianghan Bureau to oversee the Jingjiang Dike Engineering Bureau to block the breach. (5) The Yinxiangcheng Dike in Jiangling, Hubei Province, breached. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to supervise and lead the Jingjiang Dike Engineering Bureau to desperately rescue and block the breach as appropriate. (6) The Banwo section of the Jincheng Yuan in Songzi, Hubei Province, breached. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to rescue and block the breach. (7) The Mabu Guai section in Jianli, Hubei Province, breached on July 8th. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to supervise the implementation of head-wrapping works to prevent further expansion. (8) The Guhua Zhou section of the Wancheng Yuan in Jiayu, Hubei Province, breached on July 8th. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to supervise the implementation of head-wrapping works to prevent further expansion. (9) The Liuhe Yuan in Jiayu, Hubei Province, breached at midnight on July 5th, with a length of 50 meters. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to supervise the implementation of head-wrapping works. (10) The Xindi Dike in Mianyang, Hubei Province, has high water levels and a particularly dangerous situation. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to provide ample materials and supervise strict protection. (11) The main embankment below the Yongle Gate in Hanyang, Hubei Province, had water overflowing the top of the embankment and breached at 6:00 PM on July 12th. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to supervise the rapid rescue and blocking. (12) The Zhang Gong Dike in Hankou, Hubei Province, had water levels outside the dike exceeding the river level, causing collapses and extreme danger. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to work with the Hankou military and political authorities to desperately protect the dike. (13) The Chiqi Shan transverse dike in Jinkou, Hubei Province, had water levels approaching the top of the dike and was experiencing seepage. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to send personnel to the site to carry out emergency construction. (14) The Wu Hui Dike in Wuchang, Hubei Province, had high water levels and numerous locations with seepage and collapses. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to send personnel to the site to work with the Wuchang County government to vigorously protect the dike. (15) The Wanshou Guan main dike in Tuanfeng, Hubei Province, was reported on July 10th to have been washed over by the water, causing the dike to collapse for more than two zhang (approximately 6.7 meters). The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to supervise and instruct the Huanggang County government to earnestly protect the dike and find ways to block the breach.

Xiang River Situation: Strict Instructions for Rescue and Blocking

(1) The Lao Long Dike in Xiangyang, Hubei Province, had eight locations with collapses. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Engineering Bureau to work with the local county government to purchase materials nearby and carry out emergency blocking. (2) The 11th Work Site in Zhongxiang, Hubei Province, overflowed and breached on July 7th. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Bureau to supervise rapid rescue and blocking to prevent further expansion. (3) The Shuanghe Yuan in Tianmen, Hubei Province, breached at 3:30 AM on July 9th. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Bureau to supervise the implementation of head-wrapping works and rapidly proceed with blocking. (4) The Yin Jia Yuan in Hanchuan, Hubei Province, overflowed and breached at 6:00 AM on July 8th. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Bureau to supervise the implementation of head-wrapping works and find ways to block the breach. (5) The Suo Zi Yuan in Hanchuan, Hubei Province, overflowed and breached at 6:00 AM on July 8th. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Bureau to supervise the implementation of head-wrapping works and find ways to block the breach. (6) The Baofeng Yuan in Xiang Yong Dike, Caidian, Hubei Province, was reported on July 17th to have been completely overflowed and breached. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Bureau to supervise the rapid finding of ways to rescue the area. (7) The Peng Gong Yuan and Xiang Hua Yuan in Hanchuan, Hubei Province, had upstream dikes that overflowed and breached, causing western waters to flow down. They overflowed and breached at 4:00 PM on July 10th. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Bureau to supervise the effort to rescue the overflowing and breaching dikes and prevent further expansion. (8) The city dike in Hanchuan, Hubei Province, had upstream dikes that overflowed and breached, causing western waters to flow down. It overflowed and breached at 11:00 PM on July 10th. The commission has ordered the Jianghan Bureau to supervise the effort to rescue the overflowing and breaching dikes and prevent further expansion.

Repair and Defense Matters: Allocations of Funds

Regarding the repair and defense of dikes within each province, according to the unified water conservancy administrative undertaking implementation measures, the provincial governments should be responsible for planning and handling them as before. The commission previously issued instructions to the provincial governments to follow these measures. It was also stipulated that for river basins where the central government has directly affiliated water conservancy agencies, the provincial repair and defense agencies should be guided by them when handling repair and defense matters to facilitate overall planning. Subsequently, as the flood season approached, in order to ensure that the Yangtze River flood control work this year was particularly thorough, the commission specially appointed Chuan Ruilin, a member of the commission's water conservancy committee, and Mao Yisheng, director of the water conservancy department, to supervise the Yangtze River flood control matters. When it was reported that the dikes along the Jiang and Xiang Rivers were under increasing pressure, the commission, recognizing the severity of the situation, immediately sent multiple telegrams to the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission and the Jianghan Engineering Bureau, ordering their subordinates to earnestly protect the dikes. In the event of dangerous sections, they must do their best to rescue them. The commission also repeatedly sent telegrams to the provincial governments along the river, urging them to instruct their subordinates to strictly protect the dikes and not be negligent. At the same time, Qin Fen was sent with engineering personnel to inspect the flood control situation along the upper reaches of the river. Instructions were given to the flood control agencies in the areas they passed through in an effort to save the situation. Regarding the repair funds for the provinces along the river, according to the unified water conservancy administrative undertaking measures, the provinces should originally be responsible for them. However, the commission, recognizing that the Yangtze River flood control this year was unusually urgent and fearing that the provinces might be limited by their financial resources, specially allocated assistance to meet emergency needs. As of now, 100,000 yuan has been allocated for flood control, to be managed and distributed by the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission. It has been reported that the commission has transferred the funds separately based on the situation. As for the flood control funds for the main dikes of the Jiang and Xiang Rivers in Hubei Province, they are paid from the special funds for Hubei dike construction. The original budget for this year was 200,000 yuan. Now, due to the emergency of the dikes and the extremely serious situation, 500,000 yuan has been successively allocated as of now, to be managed and used by the Jianghan Engineering Bureau. At the same time, 200,000 yuan has been allocated from the dike funds to assist Hubei Province with the repair and defense of civilian dikes.

Yellow River Water Level: Exceeding Past Years

It has been found that since the beginning of July this year, there have been continuous days of rainfall in the Yellow River area. The entire river basin has been affected, especially the Luo River, Wei River, and areas near Shaanxi and Tongguan. Due to this torrential rain, the amount of water in the Yellow River has suddenly increased this month. The water levels in each river have successively exceeded the records for the same period in past years. The dikes along the river in Henan, Hebei, and Shandong provinces are therefore quite dangerous. In Dongzhuang Linpuji, Chengwu County, Shandong Province, the Tai Dike breached due to the fierce water flow, making rescue impossible. There were a total of five breaches, and the disaster situation was particularly severe. The commission has separately instructed rescue measures for all the areas reporting emergencies.

Most Counties in Western Shandong Affected

(A) The Yellow River's south bank in Shandong, between Dongzhuang and Linpuji, breached on July 10th, with a total of five breaches. The fourth breach was the largest, with a width of 180 meters. The diversion of the flow has reached 80%. The water flow is divided into two streams, flowing southeast and affecting most counties in western Shandong. The Yellow River Commission was immediately instructed by telegram to quickly implement head-wrapping and vigorously protect the Jiangsu Dike to prevent the breaches from expanding. Willow branches were also to be planted at appropriate locations to promote silt deposition and restoration. The commission also telegraphed the commission and the Shandong provincial government to quickly discuss remedial measures. At the same time, an aircraft surveying team was arranged to measure the terrain and water flow around the breaches in preparation for blocking them. (B) Henan Province: (1) The 11-kilometer section of the Guanyu Dike collapsed on July 9th, with a width of approximately 30 meters. Water has overflowed the dike and is flowing backward. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to quickly find ways to block and restore the dike. (2) At the Qinyang Work Site on the East Qin River, the water flow is directly impacting the dike, causing the base of the large dike to collapse, creating an extremely dangerous situation. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to throw stones to protect the dike. (3) At the Qinbei Sentry on the East Qin River, the protective cliff stones have sunk by two meters. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to throw stones and repair the protection. (4) At various locations such as Duicun Xiwanghe on the West Qin River, the barrages have collapsed successively. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to load and throw earth bags and boulders and to repair the barrages at any time. (5) The banks of the Kaocheng New Dike are loose and have been collapsing continuously. The remaining dike is only a little over one zhang (approximately 3.3 meters) wide. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to add retaining walls and additional low dikes. (6) At Dongba Tou, the water has reached the level of the dike. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to quickly create low dikes and throw protective boulders. (7) At Wang Xiao Zhuang and Lei Ji Zhuang and other locations, the dike has been overflowed. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to quickly create low dikes. (8) At Wubao 1, 2, and 3 in Rong Ze Xun, the foundations of the dams have shifted due to the rising water and scouring, causing one end of the three dams to shift and sink for a length of 11 meters, creating a dangerous situation. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram, and the Henan provincial government was asked to pay close attention and strictly prevent any further damage. (9) The barrage works of the Lankao Old Dike have been displaced. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to vigorously protect the dike and pay close attention to prevent any further damage. (10) At Wu Zhi, Zheng Shang, Zhong Shang, Kai Chen, Kai Bei, and other locations, the barrage works have shifted. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to vigorously repair the dikes and increase protection. (11) At Jun Li Sai Bu Dao, there has been a lot of water overflowing. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to plant willow trees and protect the dike with earth bags. (C) Hebei Province: (1) A leak has occurred at Shi Tou Zhuang in the northern section, and the water flow is turbulent. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to vigorously block the leak. (2) In the northern section 2, there are several locations where water is entering. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to add low dikes. (3) In the southern section 1, Xiao Pang Zhuang, there are two locations where leaks have occurred. The Yellow River Commission was instructed by telegram to pay close attention and rescue the area. (4) In Dongming County, the dike banks have leaks and collapses at night. The Hebei provincial government was asked to quickly rescue and block the leaks. (5) At Liu Zhuang Guan Ting, the barrages in front and behind have collapsed successively. The Yellow River Commission and the Hebei provincial government were separately telegraphed to throw large rocks and vigorously protect the dike. (6) At Jiu Gu Road, the river water is passing through the Hua Yang Dike and flowing directly into Jiu Gu Road, creating a very dangerous situation. The Yellow River Commission and the Hebei provincial government were separately telegraphed to strengthen the defense.

Disaster-Stricken Area Reaches Over Ten Counties

Regarding the repair and defense of dikes within each province, according to the unified water conservancy administrative undertaking implementation measures, the provincial governments should be responsible for planning and handling them as before. The commission previously issued instructions to the provincial governments to follow these measures. It was also stipulated that for river basins where the central government has directly affiliated water conservancy agencies, the provincial repair and defense agencies should be guided by them to facilitate overall planning. Subsequently, as the flood season approached, in order to ensure that the Yellow River flood control work this year was particularly thorough, the commission specially appointed Kong Xiangrong, a standing member of the commission's water conservancy committee, and Zheng Zhaoqing, deputy director of the water conservancy department, to supervise the Yellow River flood control matters. When the flood season arrived, the dikes along the river in Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces successively reported emergencies. The commission immediately issued instructions based on the emergency situation of the dikes reported by the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, separately instructing the implementation of rescue and salvage measures. The commission also repeatedly sent separate telegrams to the governments of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan provinces, urging them to instruct their subordinates to strictly protect the dikes and not be negligent in any way. In Chengwu County, Shandong Province, the Tai Dike between Dongzhuang and Linpuji overflowed and breached, with five breaches, and the disaster situation was particularly severe. The disaster-stricken area has reached over ten counties.

If the Main Flow Rushes South, Jiangsu Is Also Endangered

If the main flow rushes south, the Jiangsu Dike is in imminent danger. If the flow diverts into the canal and changes course to enter the sea through Xuzhou and Huai'an, then the counties in northern Jiangsu will become a watery land. Therefore, the commission has paid special attention to this and has repeatedly telegraphed the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, instructing them to quickly assess the water situation with the Shandong provincial government and carefully propose remedial measures, blocking the breaches as appropriate. The commission has also ordered the Shandong Provincial River Affairs Bureau to quickly implement head-wrapping to prevent the situation from worsening. At the same time, the commission has sent a telegram to the Shandong provincial government, urging them to do their best to rescue the area, and has sent a telegram to the Jiangsu provincial government, instructing them to order their subordinates to be on high alert to prevent the disaster from expanding. The commission has also sent Zheng Zhaoqing, the deputy director of the water conservancy department, along with engineering personnel, to the breached area to conduct on-site inspections and to discuss salvage measures with the Shandong provincial government in Jinan. According to a telegram from Deputy Director Zheng in Jinan, the water flow at the breach in the Tai Dike between Dongzhuang and Linpuji is turbulent, making surveying difficult. An aircraft will be dispatched to handle the surveying immediately.

Agreed on Measures: Blocking the Breaches as Appropriate

Yesterday, a joint telegram was received from Chairman Han Fuqu, Committee Chairman Li Yizhi, and Deputy Director Zheng Zhaoqing, stating that four measures have been agreed upon for blocking the breach in Dongzhuang: (1) The Shandong provincial government will urge the River Affairs Bureau to be responsible for blocking the breach, and the Yellow River Commission will provide assistance. (2) The national government is requested to specially allocate funds for the breach blocking work, which will be temporarily advanced jointly by the Economic Commission, Shandong Province, and relevant provinces, with the Economic Commission contributing 30%, Shandong Province contributing 20%, and the relevant provinces contributing 10%. (3) The current remedial measure is to plant willow trees to promote silt deposition, protect the Jiangsu Dike, and quickly propose a dike construction plan while preparing materials. (4) After the materials are ready, the breaches will be blocked as appropriate. This breach blocking project is extremely urgent, and the original proposals are indeed important. The requested advance funds will be fully prepared to the extent that financial resources allow. As for the Yellow River flood control funds, the commission has successively allocated 150,000 yuan to the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission for unified use as of now. The repair and defense costs for the provinces along the river should originally be borne by the provinces as before, according to the unified water conservancy administrative undertaking implementation measures. However, the disaster situation in Shandong Province is particularly severe, and funds are urgently needed. The commission has advanced 60,000 yuan to the Shandong provincial government to meet emergency needs.

Jiang Su

Eighth First Children's Day Visit to Government Offices

August 1st is Children's Day. The Children's Year Implementation Committee of this county petitioned the county government to issue an order to all government offices to raise flags and celebrate on this day, and to collect prizes for encouragement. In order to arouse children's interest, representatives of children from each school were selected to visit the government offices in the city, and they were given preferential treatment. It is reported that on that day, various party, government, military, and police agencies prepared prizes and sent them to the committee for distribution.

Establishment of Women's Education and Training Center

The county's relief center has gradually implemented relief programs, such as the establishment of material distribution centers and poverty relief centers. It is now learned that the Women's Education and Training Center has also been prepared and has renovated the old site of the handicraft training center as an office. Zhong Taishi has been appointed as the director. It is reported that due to limited funds, the center will temporarily accommodate 30 women, teaching them embroidery, sewing, housework, etc. After the training period is over, they will be matched with suitable partners.

Suzhou

Private Prostitutes in Jinmen Stop Paying Dues in Protest

The Wuxian Public Security Bureau has recently been very strict in dealing with the issue of prostitution. As a result, there have been several cases of private prostitutes being fined every day. Therefore, the general private prostitutes are very resentful. Among the private prostitutes, there is a Changzhou woman nicknamed Lao Wu, who has considerable influence. She suddenly notified all the private prostitutes outside Jinmen on the evening of the 24th to unanimously stop paying dues. At that time, those who had already taken customers returned the night fees as a protest. Because the business of the various hotels outside the gate depends entirely on private prostitutes, it is expected that the hotels will come forward to mediate after the protest. However, most of the private prostitutes are poor, and it is feared that the suspension of dues will not last long. Therefore, the Jinmen Road, which is known as a city that never sleeps, suddenly felt deserted, which is also an interesting anecdote in the crackdown on prostitution.

Wuxi

Xihu Road Opens to Traffic at the Beginning of the Month

The Xihu Highway, which was constructed by the Jiangsu Construction Department since April of last year, has been completed in all aspects. It was originally scheduled to be officially handed over to Mei Chengzhang, the director of the Xihu Road Engineering Office, on July 15th. However, Mr. Mei was in Beijing at the time, presiding over the flood control work in Beijing, and could not spare himself. Therefore, it was not implemented. Mr. Mei returned to Wuxi the day before yesterday after finishing his official duties in Beijing and handed over all the procedures of the Engineering Office to the company to take over. As for the date of the opening ceremony, it is scheduled for August 1st at the Luyang Bridge in Nanxiang. At that time, there will definitely be a grand occasion.

Eighth Branch Bureau Captures Four Thieves

The home of farmer Zhang Jinfu in Zhangqiaotou, Third District, was robbed by more than ten bandits at around 12:00 AM on April 26th of this year, suffering a loss of more than 100 yuan. The day before yesterday, Gao Shichun, the director of the Eighth Branch Bureau of Public Security in charge of the area, captured Zhang Agen, Yu Rongquan, and accomplices Xu Ashou and Xu Qisheng and other four robbers in Xiajiabian Qingqi Village and other places. They were all brought to the bureau for strict interrogation. The robbers confessed to robbing Zhang Jinfu's home, and they were immediately presented to the general bureau. Yesterday (the 25th), they were transferred to the county government for interrogation. Wu Gengshi, the director of the trial division, opened a court to interrogate them once and ordered them to be detained together pending investigation.

Jiang Zhen

Regulations for Ranks of Strong Labor Team Leaders

The Department of Civil Affairs has repeatedly received reports from various counties that the compilation of strong labor teams has been completed, and that the ranks of the leaders of each level of the strong labor teams have not yet been promulgated. In order to unify the ranks, the department has stipulated that the rank of the battalion commander is lieutenant colonel, the battalion adjutant is major, the company commander is captain, the company adjutant is lieutenant, and the platoon leader is second lieutenant. Orders have been sent to each county to follow these regulations.

High Court Branch Office Organizes Detention Center

The Fifth Branch of the High Court was formally established on the first of this month. The number of civil and criminal appeals from various counties has been increasing day by day. In order to organize the detention center, the court sent the prisoners previously held in the High Court back to Suzhou. At the same time, 30 appeal cases from various counties under the jurisdiction of the High Court were transferred to the detention center to await trial.

Haimen

Famous Drug Dealer Dies in Prison

Wei Kanghai, a famous drug dealer in this county, secretly set up a mechanism near the Elderly Hall in the west of the county city in October of the previous year to manufacture red pills. Hao, the former director of the Public Security Bureau, led the police to crack the case, and Wei and the pill-making machines and raw materials were all sent to the county and then to the Zhenjiang Garrison Command. After the facts were ascertained, he was sentenced to five years in prison and sent back to the county prison for execution in May of last year. Wei suddenly contracted erysipelas in prison. After repeated treatments, the treatments failed to work. On the 23rd, Chen, the auditor, went to the Doutian Hall for inspection and confirmed that he had died of illness. It was ordered that the Pushan Hall prepare a coffin to collect the body and wait for the family to claim it.

Nantong

Planning to Reduce Land Tax

The land tax in Tongyi is more than thirteen yuan per mu, including regular tax and surcharges, which is difficult for the people to bear. It was decided at the county administrative meeting to set up a research association to reduce land tax surcharges. Wu Jiqian and other nine people were selected as members. The first meeting is scheduled for August 1st.

The Arrival of the Dada New Ship

The Dada Shipping Company's new ship, the Dada, arrived at Tianshenggang at noon on the 23rd on its maiden voyage between Shanghai and Yangzhou. Yang Guanbei, Wang Xianglun, and other employees of the company invited local people from all walks of life to board the ship for a visit. Commissioner Zheng also attended, as well as the county magistrates of Tong, Rugao, Hai'an, Chongming, Qidong, and Jingjiang. The ship departed for Yangzhou at 5:00 PM in the evening.

Drug Trafficking Criminals Tried by Military Law

A large-scale drug trafficking organization was uncovered in Tongcheng, and more than one hundred male and female criminals were arrested. They have been sent to the district security headquarters for trial by military law. The Jiangsu Provincial Anti-Smoking Commission telegraphed Commissioner Zheng, stating that in the recent searches for drug offenders in Nantong, more than 100 people have been arrested, many of whom are major criminals. The commission praised Commissioner Zheng's effective supervision and County Magistrate Jin and Public Security Bureau Director Song for their loyalty and diligence in performing their duties and for their ability to carry out a large-scale crackdown on drugs. The commission requested that they be praised for their efforts.

Yangzhou

The River Tide Flows Backwards, and the Riverbank is Again in Danger

The water level in each section of the canal rose slightly on the 24th by one or two inches. The water level at the Yuma Tou in Gaoyou reached 4.954 meters, and the water level at the Wanjia Tang Lake was 4.860 meters. Because the southeast wind has been very strong for several days, the river tide has flowed back to Gaoyou. Therefore, the water level in the canal area of Guazhou and Yangzhou has been particularly high in recent days. Small boats have reached the towing period. It is reported that the Canal Engineering Bureau has received an order from the province that all long-distance telephones used to transmit flood prevention information in Suqian, Siyang, Huaiyin, Huai'an, Shiying, Gaoyou, Jiangdu, Lianshui, Guanyun, and Fengxian counties are allowed to connect free of charge. As for the Liuxu riverbank problem, the embankment along the coast is in imminent danger due to the strong scouring force of the southeast wind for several days. The Construction Bureau has sent personnel to be stationed at the Yangtze Bridge to test the water records every day and report them at any time so that preparations can be made.
