News

Since its organization, the Zacao Art Friends Society has received the support of comrades from all parties to join and cooperate, so the society's affairs are exceptionally solid. The harmonica and drama groups have stopped broadcasting for a month, which has caused inquiries from all walks of life. Now, the society has resolved through its eighth general meeting to move all society affairs and correspondence matters to No. 27 Huaxing Lane, Xicangqiao Street, Shanghai. In addition, the society's published "Zacao Literature and Art" weekly will continue to be edited by Xia Zhonghan and Wu Xiongjian.

Miss Yang Zengshu of the Rose Troupe went to Beijing for troupe affairs and returned to Shanghai the day before yesterday. In addition to the normal broadcast, she will continue to print the fourth issue of the Guanghua Collection to give to the audience. The saying that some tabloid said she had left is completely untrue. Because Mr. Yang is the founder and leader of the Rose Troupe, and the female members have been able to achieve today's results because they were all taught by Mr. Yang alone, so in fact there is absolutely no possibility of leaving. Moreover, the Rose Troupe is currently preparing several new songs and musical dramas, which will be broadcast soon. There are fears that there will not be enough female members to allocate, so it is planned to add several members from Ping or who can speak Mandarin. Anyone with considerable achievements can sign up. Correspondence address: Zhou Gong, 145 Chibang Road.

Movie News

Linhua Snippets

Wang Cilong's new work was originally planned to be Liang Desuo's "Dayu Ridge," but due to various reasons, it is temporarily postponed. It has now been decided to adopt an ethical and social drama written by Jin Qingyu, with the film title yet to be determined.

Cai Chusheng's new work will be sent to Beijing for review soon. It is a children's educational film, with the title yet to be determined, but it is not based on an adaptation of "Watch."

"Family" only has one more location scene left before it is completed. This film writes about four generations of the same family living together, running through decades of stories. The whole play is full of family love, but it is definitely not promoting a narrow family concept.

Since the film "Family" has been completed, Chen Yanyan has been focusing on the work of "Wild Geese Falling on the Cold River." This film was specially written for Yanyan by Ma Xu Weibang, and it is expected that Yanyan will make a special contribution.

Since starring in "Carefree Gentleman," Mei Lin has received enthusiastic attention from the audience. Mei Lin also plays an important role in "Family."

"Family" is a collaboration between twelve Linhua stars, and each actor has an equal opportunity for development.

When Wang Cilong's new work begins filming, he will lead the photography team to Nankou to take scenes. Sun Yu and Wu Yonggang's new works will take scenes in Qingdao.

Xi Zhihua plays Chen Yanyan's younger aunt in "Wild Geese Falling on the Cold River," talkative and vivid, almost making Yanyan angry to death.

"Four Sisters" and "Wild Geese Falling on the Cold River" are both working very hard, and "Family" and other three films will be released one after another following "Little Angel."

Famous Young Composer Nie Er Dies in Sea Bath in Japan

Famous young composer Mr. Nie Er went to Japan this spring to prepare for a short-term inspection and then went to Europe to study music. He asked a friend to get his last letter, which said that he would go to Kyoto, Osaka, and Kobe on July 17 to participate in the Japanese "New Association" tour performance. Unexpectedly, according to another friend's report, he died after being swept away by a wave while swimming in the sea in Fujizawa Town, Kanagawa Prefecture, Japan on the 17th. His body was missing. The colleagues of the Telecommunications Universal News Agency will publish the following notice in its sixth issue of the pictorial, "Young composer Mr. Nie Er died on July 17 while swimming in the sea in Kugenuma, Fujizawa Town, Kanagawa Prefecture, Japan. Most of the colleagues of this newspaper have known Mr. Nie Er, and the bad news has caused great grief. It is planned to open a special column in the seventh issue of this newspaper to commemorate the author of this epoch-making Chinese film music. There are many friends of Mr. Nie Er in all parties. If you are willing to offer condemnations, it will not only mourn the untimely death of a genius, but also promote the quiet light of the spring. Please send your pieces to the editorial office at No. 405 Jingzhou Road before August 10." It is said that the former friends of Nie Er are now preparing a memorial service for him, and are collecting his posthumous works to hold a performance to mourn him. His works, such as Graduation Song, Pioneer of the Road, Great Road Song, New Woman Song, Flying Flower Song, Song of the Singing Girl Under the Iron Heel, March of the Volunteers, are mostly popular and do not need to be introduced. This is indeed a major misfortune for the Chinese film music industry.

Nie Er's Remains

Public Screening of "The Secret of the Dog Racing Track"

"The Secret of the Dog Racing Track" is a new and unique product from the British Gaumont-British company. Dog racing originated in England, so a film produced by an English company and capturing the local scenery of England will naturally be of excellent quality. The dogs participating in the race in the film can be said to be a grand spectacle of the nation, especially since Mick The Miller, famous throughout Europe, displays his skills and performs various acts here. (Mick is a famous animal with documented records and is a highly revered idol in the English dog racing scene; his parents are both of excellent breeding stock). Collaborating actors include comedic stars Sonny Hale, Wynes Lloyd, etc. This film is not only recommended by art and entertainment enthusiasts but is also a masterpiece that dog racing fans cannot miss. It is currently being screened in "Nanjing."

Recent News from Yanguang

Since its establishment, the Yanguang Film and Drama Society has been employing domestic researchers in dramatic arts for guidance, specializing in the study of spoken drama. Recently, they are planning to stage the five-act comedy "She Stoops to Conquer" by Oliver Goldsmith. It is said that they are still lacking several male and female actors. Any male or female comrades with proper cultivation in drama are welcome to apply to participate. The society's address is temporarily located in the French Concession, at the end of Nanking Road, Rong Sheng Li.
